 vrath or tyohaar nai prerana evam sphurti kaa sanvahan karte hai

e
 Gudipadwa, Akhatij or Akshaya Tritiya, Pradosha of Dussehra and Deepavali
 Date
 bhartiya lok-maanas sadaiv se ritu parv manaata rahaa he
 a series of fasts, festivals and festivals are constantly tied to folk life to celebrate the change of seasons with auspiciousness
 isi shrinkhalaa main akshay tritiya kaa parv vasant or greeshm ke sandhikaal kaa mahotsav he
 The fast-festival celebrated on Vaishakh Shukla Tritiya is very popular and popular in the world
 vishnu dharmasutra, matsay puraana, naarad puraana tathaa bhavishya puraana main iskaa vistrut ullekh kiya gaya he tathaa isaki kai kathaayen prachlit he
 Sanatan righteous public householders celebrate it with great enthusiasm
 akshay tritiya ko die gaye daan or kiye gaye snaan, jap, havan aadi karmon kaa shubh or anant fal miltaa he
 According to the Bhavishya Purana, the fruit of all karmas becomes Akshay, hence its name Akshay
 is baar akshay tritiya buudhvaar 18 april 2018 ko he
 The sunrise will last from 3:03 pm
 baishakh maas ke shukla paksh kii tritiya ko akshay tritiya yaa akhatij kehete hai
 The literal meaning of Akshay is never decayed, that is to remain permanent
 sthai vahiin rah saktaa jo sarvada satya he
 It can be said with certainty that truth is only the divine which is renewable, unbroken and comprehensive
 yah akshay tritiya tithi ishwar tithi he
 This Akshaya Tithi is also called Parshuram Tithi because it is Parshuram's birthday
 parashuram ji kii ginati mahatmaon main kii jaati he
 Hence, this date is also called Chiranjeevi Tithi
 chaaron yugon satyuga, tretayug, dwaparayug or kalyug main se treta yug kaa aarambh isi akhatij se hua he
 Tretayug has started on Akshaya Tritiya
 jisase is tithi ko yug kii aarambh kii tithi 'yugaditithi' bhi kehete hai
 Keep these things in the purse, there will never be a shortage of money, on the auspicious Tritiya, one of the four pilgrimage shrines opens the doors of Lord Sreebadrinarayan
 darshanathiyon evam bhakton kii apaar bheed rahati he
 The charitable work done by devotees on this day, renunciation, donation-dakshina, home-havan, Ganga bath etc
 are counted in Akshay
 bhagwaan bhakton kaa prasad prem se grahan karte hai
 Akshaya Tritiya takes place once a year in Vrindavan at the feet of Shri Bihari Ji
 desh ke kone-kone se shraddhalu bhakt charan darshan ke liye vrundavan padhaarte hai
 This day of introspection and introspection is inspiring us to brainstorm, self-discipline and observation
 yah din 'nij manu mukuru sudhaari' kaa din he
 It is the day of renewable work in place of the works of decay
 is din hamen dekhnaa-samajhnaa hoga ki bhautik rup se dikhaai dene vaala yah sthool sharir or sansar kii samast vastuon se kshaydharma he, akshay dharma nahin hai
 Aphrodisiac things create impudence, impure thoughts, ego, selfishness, work, anger and greed which Lord Krishna has called devilish instinct in the Gita
 jabaki akshayadharma sakaaratmak chintan- manan hamen daivisampada kii ore le jaataa he
 We attain ultimate peace by renunciation, benevolence, friendship, compassion and love, that is, we attain divine qualities
 is drushti se yah tithi hamen jivan mulyon kaa varnan karne kaa sandesh detii he- satyamev jayate kii ore agrasar karti he
 Akshaya Tritiya is a day of social festivals
 is din koi doosraa muhoort naa dekh kar swayan siddh abhijit shubh muhoort ke kaaran vivaah utsav aadi mangalik kaary sampann kiye jate hai
 The Gita itself is a renewable, immortal Nidhi Granth
 jiskaa pathan-pathan, manan evam swadhyay karke ham jivan kii purnataa ko paa sakate hai
 Can understand the significance of life and achieve the renewable element
 akshay ke samaan hamaara sankalp drudh, shraddhapurna evam hamaari nishtha atoot honi chahie
 Only then we can get the overall spiritual fruits of fasting, fasting migrants
 shaastra main ullekith he ki aaj ke din swarna kii kharidari bhi kerani chahie
 Money is formed
 dhan-sampada main vruddhi kaa yoga bhi banataa he
 Whatever work a person does on this day, it becomes renewable
 isliye dharmik evam shubh kaary aaj ke din jarur karnaa chahie
 Posthumously, a person is freed from the bondage of life and death and attains Vaikuntha Loka
 amarnath yatra par jane vaale kai shraddhaluon kii swasthya sambandhi samasyaon ke kaaran har saal maut ke badhate maamalon ko dekhte hue yatra kaa prabandhan karne vaale shrin board ne faisla kiya he ki ab se yatra ke liye panjikaran karaane ke samay shraddhaluon ko chikitsa praaanpatr dikhaanaa hoga

 is baithak kii adhyakshata rajyapal enen vohara ne kii

 pravaktaa ne kaha, ‘board ne hriday sambandhi samasyaon ke kaaran maare jane vaale shraddhaluon kii badhati sankhya par charchaa kii

 Ekadashi date of Jyeshtha Shukla Paksha is called Nirjala Ekadashi
 bhim ne ek maatr isi upwas ko rakhaa tha or moorchhit ho gaye the, atah isko bhimseni ekadshi bhi kaha jaataa he
 By fasting without water on this day, the virtues of all the eleventh years of the year are attained
 iske alaava dharm, arth, kaam or moksh , chaaron purushaarthon kii prapti bhi hoti he
 On this day, wishes of good health and a pleasant life can be fulfilled
 is baar nirjala ekadshi kaa vrath 23 june ko rakhaa jayega
 What is the method of fasting for Nirjala Ekadashi? - Take a bath in the morning and offer water to the Sun God
 - iske baad pile vastra dhaaran karke bhagwaan vishnu kii puja karen
 - Offer them yellow flowers, panchamrit and tulsi dal
 - iske baad shri hari or maan lakshmi ke mantron kaa jaap karen 
 - Donate water, food, or shoes to a poor person
 - aaj ke din vaise to nirjal upwas hi rakkha jaataa he ,- parantu aavashyaktaa hone par jaleey aahaar or falahar liya ja saktaa he
 What to do on Nirjala Ekadashi? - Take fast on this day only by consuming water and fruits- Worship your Guru or Lord Vishnu in the morning and in the evening - If you must worship Shri Hari by awakening at night - Chanting more and more time on this day And keep in mind - Donating water and water vessels will be a special blessing, how to end the fast of Nirjala Ekadashi?
